                            var kpiCells = tempDiv.querySelectorAll('.kpi .v');
                            if (kpiCells.length &gt;= 2) {
                                totalTasks = parseInt(kpiCells[0].textContent, 10) || 0;
                                totalWeight = parseInt(kpiCells[1].textContent, 10) || 0;
                            }
                        } catch (e) {
                            // Ignore parse errors
                        }
                    }

                    return {
                        hoTen: row.HovaTen || '',
                        msnv: row.MSNV || '',
                        phongBan: row.PhongBan || '',
                        month: month,
                        submittedAt: row.NVDuyet || '',
                        signStatus: signStatus,
                        totalTasks: totalTasks,
                        totalWeight: totalWeight,
                        idTongKet: row.IDTongKet || row.idTongKet || ''
                    };
                });
            }

            // Helper: Build payload for NoiDungTongKet API
            function buildTongKetPayloadForNoiDung(empMeta, idTongKet, monthParts) {
                return {
                    YeuCauTongKet: 'NoiDungTongKet',
                    HovaTen: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.HovaTen ? String(empMeta.HovaTen) : '',
                    MSNV: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.MSNV ? String(empMeta.MSNV) : '',
                    Email: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.Email ? String(empMeta.Email) : '',
                    EmailQuanLy: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.EmailQuanLy ? String(empMeta.EmailQuanLy) : '',
                    CongTy: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.CongTy ? String(empMeta.CongTy) : '',
                    ChiNhanh: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.ChiNhanh ? String(empMeta.ChiNhanh) : '',
                    PhongBan: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.PhongBan ? String(empMeta.PhongBan) : '',
                    ChucVu: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.ChucVu ? String(empMeta.ChucVu) : '',
                    NVDuyet: '',
                    QLDuyet: '',
                    TongKet: '',
                    Thang: monthParts &amp;&amp; monthParts.Thang ? String(monthParts.Thang) : '',
                    Nam: monthParts &amp;&amp; monthParts.Nam ? String(monthParts.Nam) : '',
                    IDTongKet: idTongKet || ''
                };
            }

            // Helper: Extract TongKet HTML from response
            function extractTongKetHtml(res) {
                if (!res) return '';
                // Case 1: String directly
                if (typeof res === 'string') return res;
                // Case 2: res.TongKet
                if (res.TongKet) return res.TongKet;
                // Case 3: res.body is string JSON
                if (res.body &amp;&amp; typeof res.body === 'string') {
                    try {
                        var parsed = JSON.parse(res.body);
                        if (parsed.TongKet) return parsed.TongKet;
                        if (parsed.body &amp;&amp; parsed.body.TongKet) return parsed.body.TongKet;
                    } catch (e) {
                        // Ignore
                    }
                }
                // Case 4: res.body.TongKet
                if (res.body &amp;&amp; res.body.TongKet) return res.body.TongKet;
                // Case 5: Array
                if (Array.isArray(res) &amp;&amp; res.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; res[0].TongKet) {
                    return res[0].TongKet;
                }
                return '';
            }

            // Helper: Build payload for Duyet (NV or QL)
            function buildTongKetPayloadForDuyet(role, empMeta, idTongKet, monthParts, tongKetHtmlOpt) {
                return {
                    YeuCauTongKet: role === 'NV' ? 'NVDuyetTongKet' : 'QLDuyetTongKet',
                    HovaTen: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.HovaTen ? String(empMeta.HovaTen) : '',
                    MSNV: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.MSNV ? String(empMeta.MSNV) : '',
                    Email: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.Email ? String(empMeta.Email) : '',
                    EmailQuanLy: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.EmailQuanLy ? String(empMeta.EmailQuanLy) : '',
                    CongTy: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.CongTy ? String(empMeta.CongTy) : '',
                    ChiNhanh: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.ChiNhanh ? String(empMeta.ChiNhanh) : '',
                    PhongBan: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.PhongBan ? String(empMeta.PhongBan) : '',
                    ChucVu: empMeta &amp;&amp; empMeta.ChucVu ? String(empMeta.ChucVu) : '',
                    NVDuyet: role === 'NV' ? 'XacNhan' : '',
                    QLDuyet: role === 'QL' ? 'XacNhan' : '',
                    TongKet: tongKetHtmlOpt || '',
                    Thang: monthParts &amp;&amp; monthParts.Thang ? String(monthParts.Thang) : '',
                    Nam: monthParts &amp;&amp; monthParts.Nam ? String(monthParts.Nam) : '',
                    IDTongKet: idTongKet || ''
                };
            }

            async function loadSummaryList() {
                // Validate employee meta
                var empMeta = getEmployeeMetaForWork();
                if (!empMeta || !empMeta.MSNV) {
                    showToast('Chưa có thông tin nhân viên', 'warn', 2500);
                    return;
                }

                // Get selected month
                var kpiMonthEl = byId('kpiMonth');
                var selectedMonth = kpiMonthEl ? kpiMonthEl.value : '';
                if (!selectedMonth) {
                    showToast('Vui lòng chọn tháng KPI', 'warn', 2500);
                    return;
                }

                var monthParts = getSelectedYearMonthParts(selectedMonth);

                // Build payload
                var payload = buildTongKetPayloadForDanhSach(empMeta, monthParts);
                logDebug('[DANHSACH_TONGKET] Calling API with payload:', JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2));

                try {
                    var raw = await callTongKetSignApi(payload);
                    var rows = parseTongKetResponse(raw);
                    logDebug('[DANHSACH_TONGKET] Raw rows:', rows.length);

                    state.summaries = mapTongKetRowsToSummaries(rows).sort(function(a, b) {
                        return String(b.month).localeCompare(String(a.month));
                    });
                renderSummaries();
                } catch (err) {
                    logError('[DANHSACH_TONGKET] Error:', err);
                    showToast('Không tải được danh sách tổng kết: ' + (err.message || ''), 'error', 3500);
                }
            }

            // Tab Công Việc: KHÔNG tự động tải tasks khi reload - user phải bấm nút
            async function reloadAll() {
                try {
                    await loadEmployeeAndGroups();
                    setMonthState(byId('kpiMonth').value || getCurrentMonth());
                    // Chỉ load summary list, KHÔNG load tasks - user phải bấm "Tải công việc"
                    await loadSummaryList();
                    showToast('Đã tải lại dữ liệu', 'success');
                } catch (err) {
                    logError(err);
                    showToast(err.message || 'Không tải được dữ liệu', 'error', 3500);
                }
            }

            function setMonthState(ym) {
                state.selectedMonth = ym;
                state.isLockedMonth = isPastMonth(ym);
                var kpiMonthEl = byId('kpiMonth');
                if (kpiMonthEl) kpiMonthEl.value = ym;
                renderLockBadge();
            }

            // Load tasks for Tổng Kết tab using YeuCau = TongKet (HovaTen, MSNV, ChucVu, PhongBan, ChiNhanh, CongTy, Thang, Nam)
            async function loadTongKetTasks() {
                var kpiMonthEl = byId('kpiMonth');
                var selectedMonth = kpiMonthEl ? kpiMonthEl.value : '';
                if (!selectedMonth) {
                    showToast('Vui lòng chọn tháng KPI', 'warn', 2500);
                    return;
                }

                if (!(state.employee &amp;&amp; state.employee.msnv)) {
                    showToast('Chưa có thông tin nhân viên', 'warn', 2500);
                    return;
                }

                var empMeta = getEmployeeMetaForWork();
                var monthParts = getSelectedYearMonthParts(selectedMonth);

                // API payload: YeuCau = TongKet with HovaTen, MSNV, ChucVu, PhongBan, ChiNhanh, CongTy, Thang, Nam
                var payload = {
                    YeuCau: toApiString('TongKet'),
                    HovaTen: toApiString(empMeta.HovaTen),
                    MSNV: toApiString(empMeta.MSNV),
                    ChucVu: toApiString(empMeta.ChucVu || ''),
                    PhongBan: toApiString(empMeta.PhongBan),
                    ChiNhanh: toApiString(empMeta.ChiNhanh),
                    CongTy: toApiString(empMeta.CongTy),
                    Email: toApiString(empMeta.Email || ''),
                    EmailQuanLy: toApiString(empMeta.EmailQuanLy || ''),
                    Thang: toApiString(monthParts.Thang),
                    Nam: toApiString(monthParts.Nam)
                };

                logDebug('[TONGKET] Loading tasks with payload:', JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2));

                try {
                    var rawData = await callCongViecApi(payload);
                    var rows = parseCongViecResponse(rawData);

                    logDebug('[TONGKET] Raw API rows:', rows.length);

                    // Store raw rows for Tổng Kết (raw API response)
                    state.tongketTasks = rows;

                    // Show table and render
                    var tableWrap = byId('tongketTaskTableWrap');
                    if (tableWrap) tableWrap.style.display = 'block';

                    // Render the task list table
                    renderTongKetTasks(rows);

                    // Update info text
                    var tongketInfoText = byId('tongketInfoText');
                    if (tongketInfoText) {
                        tongketInfoText.textContent = 'Đã tải ' + rows.length + ' công việc';
                    }

                    // Enable summary button after load
                    var btnSummarySubmit = byId('btnSummarySubmit');
                    if (btnSummarySubmit) btnSummarySubmit.disabled = false;

                    showToast('Đã tải ' + rows.length + ' công việc', 'success', 2000);

                } catch (err) {
                    logError('[TONGKET] Error loading tasks:', err);
                    showToast('Không tải được công việc: ' + (err.message || 'Lỗi không xác định'), 'error', 3500);
                }
            }

            // Render task list for Tổng Kết tab (giống tab Công Việc)
            function renderTongKetTasks(tasks) {
                var tbody = byId('tongketTaskTableBody');
                if (!tbody) {
                    logWarn('renderTongKetTasks: tbody not found');
                    return;
                }

                tbody.innerHTML = '';

                if (!tasks || !tasks.length) {
                    tbody.innerHTML = '&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td colspan="6" class="text-center muted"&gt;Không có công việc nào&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;';
                    return;
                }

                // Group tasks by NhomCongViec
                var groups = {};
                tasks.forEach(function(t) {
                    var groupName = t.NhomCongViec || '(Chưa phân nhóm)';
                    if (!groups[groupName]) {
                        groups[groupName] = [];
                    }
                    groups[groupName].push(t);
                });

                // Sort groups by name
                var sortedGroupNames = Object.keys(groups).sort();

                // Render each group
                sortedGroupNames.forEach(function(groupName) {
                    var groupTasks = groups[groupName];
                    var taskCount = groupTasks.length;

                    // Render group row
                    var groupTr = document.createElement('tr');
                    groupTr.className = 'group-row';
                    groupTr.innerHTML = '&lt;td colspan="6"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;' + escapeHtml(groupName) + ' (' + taskCount + ')&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/td&gt;';
                    tbody.appendChild(groupTr);

                    // Render tasks in this group
                    groupTasks.forEach(function(t, idx) {
                        var tr = document.createElement('tr');
                        var stt = idx + 1;
                        var congViec = t.CongViec || '';
                        var thoiHan = t.ThoiHan || '';
                        var trangThai = t.TrangThai || 'Mới';
                        var dienGiai = t.DienGiaiKetQua || '-';
                        var taiLieu = t.TaiLieu || '';
                        var taiLieuHtml = taiLieu
                            ? '&lt;a href="' + escapeHtml(taiLieu) + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="btn btn-soft btn-icon" title="Tài liệu"&gt;&lt;i class="fa fa-paperclip"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;'
                            : '-';

                        tr.innerHTML =
                            '&lt;td&gt;' + stt + '&lt;/td&gt;' +
                            '&lt;td&gt;' + escapeHtml(congViec) + '&lt;/td&gt;' +
                            '&lt;td&gt;' + escapeHtml(thoiHan) + '&lt;/td&gt;' +
                            '&lt;td&gt;' + renderStatusBadge(trangThai) + '&lt;/td&gt;' +
                            '&lt;td&gt;' + escapeHtml(dienGiai) + '&lt;/td&gt;' +
                            '&lt;td&gt;' + taiLieuHtml + '&lt;/td&gt;';
                        tbody.appendChild(tr);
                    });
                });
            }

            // ===== CSV Utilities =====
            // CSV parser (used by Upload .csv)
            function parseCsv(text) {
                var rows = [];
                var row = [];
                var cur = '';
                var i = 0;
                var inQuotes = false;

                while (i &lt; text.length) {
                    var ch = text[i];
                    if (inQuotes) {
                        if (ch === '"') {
                            if (text[i + 1] === '"') { cur += '"'; i += 2; continue; }
                            inQuotes = false; i++; continue;
                        }
                        cur += ch; i++; continue;
                    }

                    if (ch === '"') { inQuotes = true; i++; continue; }
                    if (ch === ',') { row.push(cur); cur = ''; i++; continue; }
                    if (ch === '\n') { row.push(cur); rows.push(row); row = []; cur = ''; i++; continue; }
                    if (ch === '\r') { i++; continue; }
                    cur += ch; i++;
                }
                row.push(cur);
                if (row.length &gt; 1 || row[0] !== '') rows.push(row);
                return rows;
            }

            // ===== Event Bindings =====
            function bindEvents() {
                // Tabs - với null guard cho tab pane
                document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(function(x) { x.classList.remove('active'); });
                        document.querySelectorAll('.tab-pane').forEach(function(x) { x.classList.remove('active'); });
                        btn.classList.add('active');
                        var targetTab = byId(btn.dataset.tab);
                        if (targetTab) targetTab.classList.add('active');
                    });
                });

                var btnReloadAll = byId('btnReloadAll');
                if (btnReloadAll) btnReloadAll.addEventListener('click', reloadAll);

                var kpiMonthEl = byId('kpiMonth');
                if (kpiMonthEl) {
                    kpiMonthEl.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
                        setMonthState(e.target.value);
                        resetTaskForm();
                        // KHÔNG tự động tải công việc - user phải bấm nút "Tải công việc"
                    });
                }

                var btnLoadTasks = byId('btnLoadTasks');
                if (btnLoadTasks) btnLoadTasks.addEventListener('click', loadTasksBySelected);

                var btnLoadTongKetTasks = byId('btnLoadTongKetTasks');
                if (btnLoadTongKetTasks) btnLoadTongKetTasks.addEventListener('click', loadTongKetTasks);

                var btnResetTask = byId('btnResetTask');
                if (btnResetTask) btnResetTask.addEventListener('click', resetTaskForm);

                // Event listener cho Từ ngày - cập nhật min của Đến ngày
                var taskDateFromEl = byId('taskDateFrom');
                var taskDateToEl = byId('taskDateTo');
                if (taskDateFromEl) {
                    taskDateFromEl.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
                        if (taskDateToEl &amp;&amp; e.target.value) {
                            taskDateToEl.min = e.target.value;
                            // Nếu Đến ngày nhỏ hơn Từ ngày thì reset về Từ ngày
                            if (taskDateToEl.value &amp;&amp; taskDateToEl.value &lt; e.target.value) {
                                taskDateToEl.value = e.target.value;
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }

                // Validate file type on selection
                var taskAttachmentEl = byId('taskAttachment');
                if (taskAttachmentEl) {
                    taskAttachmentEl.addEventListener('change', function() {
                        // [MULTI_FILE_TODO] Add selected files to queue
                        addSelectedFiles(taskAttachmentEl.files);
                        // Clear input value to allow re-selecting same file
                        taskAttachmentEl.value = '';
                    });
                }

                var taskForm = byId('taskForm');
                if (taskForm) {
                    taskForm.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();

                        // [SUBMIT_FLOW_BEGIN]

                        // [GUARD] Chống double submit - nếu đang submit thì bỏ qua
                        if (state.isSubmittingTask) {
                            showToast('Đang xử lý, vui lòng chờ...', 'warn', 2000);
                            return;
                        }

                        // [GUARD] Lấy originalBtnText TRƯỚC khi lock UI
                        var btnSaveTask = byId('btnSaveTask');
                        var originalBtnText = btnSaveTask ? btnSaveTask.innerHTML : 'Lưu công việc';

                        // [GUARD] Lock UI trước khi bắt đầu submit
                        lockTaskSubmitUI();

                        try {
                            if (state.isLockedMonth) throw new Error('Tháng đã khóa, không thể thêm/sửa công việc');

                            // Validate: kiểm tra đã chọn việc từ dropdown
                            var viecSelectEl = byId('viecSelect');
                            var selectedViecValue = viecSelectEl ? viecSelectEl.value : '';
                            if (!selectedViecValue) {
                                throw new Error('Vui lòng chọn việc cần làm từ danh sách');
                            }

                            var taskIdEl = byId('taskId');
                            var taskTitleEl = byId('taskTitle');
                            var taskTargetEl = byId('taskTarget');
                            var taskDateFromEl = byId('taskDateFrom');
                            var taskDateToEl = byId('taskDateTo');
                            var taskStatusEl = byId('taskStatus');
                            var taskAttachmentUrlEl = byId('taskAttachmentUrl');
                            var workGroupDisplayEl = byId('workGroupDisplay');
                            var workGroupSelectEl = byId('workGroupSelect');

                            // Lấy thông tin từ meta đã lưu
                            var selectedMeta = state.bieuMauWorkMap ? state.bieuMauWorkMap[selectedViecValue] : null;
                            if (!selectedMeta || !selectedMeta.idNhom) {
                                throw new Error('Biểu mẫu thiếu thông tin nhóm công việc cho việc đã chọn');
                            }
                            // NEW: Sync selectedGroupId từ selectedMeta
                            state.selectedGroupId = String(selectedMeta.idNhom || '');

                            // Lấy group info từ workGroups để dùng trong payload
                            var group = state.workGroups ? state.workGroups.find(function(g) { return String(g.id) === String(state.selectedGroupId); }) : null;

                            var viecCanLam = selectedMeta ? (selectedMeta.viecText || '') : (taskTitleEl ? taskTitleEl.value.trim() : '');
                            var nhomCongViec = selectedMeta ? (selectedMeta.nhomText || '') : (workGroupDisplayEl ? workGroupDisplayEl.value : '');
                            var idNhomCongViec = selectedMeta ? (selectedMeta.idNhom || '') : (workGroupSelectEl ? workGroupSelectEl.value : '');

                            // Lấy Tỷ Trọng
                            var tyTrongEl = byId('workTyTrong');
                            var tyTrongValue = tyTrongEl ? tyTrongEl.value : '';

// [MULTI_FILE_TODO] Validate file from taskFileState (not from input.files)
                            // Kiểm tra file vượt quá 1GB
                            var filesToUpload = taskFileState.items.filter(function(item) {
                                return item.source === 'new' &amp;&amp; !item.markedForDelete;
                            });
                            for (var fidx = 0; fidx &lt; filesToUpload.length; fidx++) {
                                if (filesToUpload[fidx].size &gt; MAX_TASK_FILE_SIZE_BYTES) {
                                    throw new Error('File "' + filesToUpload[fidx].name + '" vượt quá 1GB');
                                }
                                // Validate file type
                                var v = validateAllowedOfficeFile({name: filesToUpload[fidx].name});
                                if (!v.ok) {
                                    showToast(v.message, 'error', 5000);
                                    throw new Error(v.message);
                                }
                            }

                            var fromDate = taskDateFromEl ? taskDateFromEl.value : '';
                            var toDate = taskDateToEl ? taskDateToEl.value : '';

                            // Validate: nếu nhập 1 trong 2 ngày thì phải nhập đủ cả 2
                            if ((fromDate &amp;&amp; !toDate) || (!fromDate &amp;&amp; toDate)) {
                                throw new Error('Vui lòng nhập đủ cả "Từ ngày" và "Đến ngày"');
                            }

                            // Validate: from &lt;= to
                            if (fromDate &amp;&amp; toDate &amp;&amp; fromDate &gt; toDate) {
                                throw new Error('"Từ ngày" không được lớn hơn "Đến ngày"');
                            }

                            // Kết hợp 2 trường date thành chuỗi "dd/mm/yyyy - dd/mm/yyyy" cho API
                            var thoiHan = formatDateRangeForApi(fromDate, toDate);

                            // Validate: Tên công việc không được để trống
                            var taskTitleValue = taskTitleEl ? taskTitleEl.value.trim() : '';
                            if (!taskTitleValue) {
                                throw new Error('Tên công việc không được để trống');
                            }

                            // Xác định mode: update nếu taskId đã có giá trị hợp lệ
                            var taskIdVal = (taskIdEl &amp;&amp; taskIdEl.value || '').trim();
                            var isUpdate = !!taskIdVal &amp;&amp; taskIdVal !== '0';
                            var idCongViec = null;

                            if (isUpdate) {
                                // [SUBMIT_FLOW_UPDATE_BRANCH]
                                // EDIT mode: dùng taskIdVal sẵn có, KHÔNG gọi saveTask để lấy ID

                                idCongViec = taskIdVal;

                                var updateTitle = toApiString(taskTitleEl ? taskTitleEl.value.trim() : '');
                                if (!updateTitle) throw new Error('Tên công việc không được để trống');

                                // Bước 1: XoaTaiLieu + ThemTaiLieu (batch 5 song song) qua processTaskAttachments
                                await processTaskAttachments(idCongViec, 'update');

                                // Bước 2: Build lại IDTaiLieu sau khi upload xong
                                var finalTaiLieuIds = buildTaiLieuIdsForTask();

                                // Bước 3: Gọi SuaCongViec đúng 1 lần với IDTaiLieu đã cập nhật (không dùng TaiLieu names nữa)
                                var updatePayload = {
                                    id: idCongViec,
                                    groupId: toApiString(state.selectedGroupId),
                                    groupName: toApiString(group &amp;&amp; group.name),
                                    ViecCanLam: toApiString(viecCanLam),
                                    NhomCongViec: toApiString(nhomCongViec),
                                    IDNhomCongViec: toApiString(idNhomCongViec),
                                    TyTrong: toApiString(tyTrongValue),
                                    title: updateTitle,
                                    target: toApiString(taskTargetEl ? taskTargetEl.value.trim() : ''),
                                    thoiHan: toApiString(thoiHan),
                                    status: toApiString(taskStatusEl ? taskStatusEl.value : 'Mới'),
                                    IDTaiLieu: toApiString(finalTaiLieuIds)
                                };
                                await service.saveTask(state.employee.msnv, state.selectedMonth, updatePayload);
                            } else {
                                // [SUBMIT_FLOW_CREATE_BRANCH]
                                // CREATE mode: tạo task mới
                                // Bước 1: Tạo task không có file để lấy IDCongViec
                                var initialPayload = {
                                    id: uid(),
                                    groupId: toApiString(state.selectedGroupId),
                                    groupName: toApiString(group &amp;&amp; group.name),
                                    ViecCanLam: toApiString(viecCanLam),
                                    NhomCongViec: toApiString(nhomCongViec),
                                    IDNhomCongViec: toApiString(idNhomCongViec),
                                    TyTrong: toApiString(tyTrongValue),
                                    title: toApiString(taskTitleEl ? taskTitleEl.value.trim() : ''),
                                    target: toApiString(taskTargetEl ? taskTargetEl.value.trim() : ''),
                                    thoiHan: toApiString(thoiHan),
                                    status: toApiString(taskStatusEl ? taskStatusEl.value : 'Mới'),
                                    IDTaiLieu: ''
                                };
                                if (!initialPayload.title) throw new Error('Tên công việc không được để trống');

                                var saveRes = await service.saveTask(state.employee.msnv, state.selectedMonth, initialPayload);
                                idCongViec = extractIdCongViecFromCreateResponse(saveRes) || extractIdCongViecFromSaveResult(saveRes);

                                if (!idCongViec) {
                                    var raw = (saveRes &amp;&amp; saveRes.result) ? saveRes.result : saveRes;
                                    showToast('Không lấy được ID. Response=' + String(raw &amp;&amp; raw.body ? raw.body : raw).slice(0, 120), 'warn', 4500);
                                    throw new Error('Không lấy được ID công việc từ server');
                                }

                                // Bước 2: Upload files sau khi có IDCongViec
                                await processTaskAttachments(idCongViec, 'create');

                                // Bước 3: Build lại IDTaiLieu sau khi upload xong
                                var finalTaiLieuNames = buildTaiLieuNamesForTask();
                                var finalTaiLieuIds = buildTaiLieuIdsForTask();

                                // Bước 4: Gọi SuaCongViec 1 lần để ghi IDTaiLieu vào record
                                var createFinalPayload = {
                                    id: String(idCongViec),
                                    groupId: toApiString(state.selectedGroupId),
                                    groupName: toApiString(group &amp;&amp; group.name),
                                    ViecCanLam: toApiString(viecCanLam),
                                    NhomCongViec: toApiString(nhomCongViec),
                                    IDNhomCongViec: toApiString(idNhomCongViec),
                                    TyTrong: toApiString(tyTrongValue),
                                    title: toApiString(taskTitleEl ? taskTitleEl.value.trim() : ''),
                                    target: toApiString(taskTargetEl ? taskTargetEl.value.trim() : ''),
                                    thoiHan: toApiString(thoiHan),
                                    status: toApiString(taskStatusEl ? taskStatusEl.value : 'Mới'),
                                    IDTaiLieu: toApiString(finalTaiLieuIds)
                                };
                                await service.saveTask(state.employee.msnv, state.selectedMonth, createFinalPayload);
                            }

                            // Reload tasks
                            await loadTasksBySelected();
                            resetTaskForm();

                            showToast('Đã lưu công việc', 'success');

                            // [SUBMIT_FLOW_END]
                        } catch (err) {
                            logError(err);
                            showToast(err.message || 'Lưu công việc thất bại', 'error', 3500);
                        } finally {
                            // [GUARD] Unlock UI - always
                            unlockTaskSubmitUI(originalBtnText);
                        }
                    });
                }

                var taskTableBody = byId('taskTableBody');
                if (taskTableBody) {
                    // Collapse/Expand functionality for group headers
                    taskTableBody.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        var headerRow = e.target.closest('.group-header');
                        if (headerRow) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            var g1 = headerRow.dataset.g1 || '';
                            var g2 = headerRow.dataset.g2 || '';
                            toggleGroup(g1, g2, headerRow);
                            return;
                        }
                    });

                    // Task edit/delete functionality
                    taskTableBody.addEventListener('click', async function(e) {
                        // [MULTI_FILE_TODO] Xử lý click nút xem tài liệu
                        var taiLieuBtn = e.target.closest('.btn-view-tai-lieu');
                        if (taiLieuBtn) {
                            var idCongViec = taiLieuBtn.dataset.idCongViec;
                            if (idCongViec) {
                                showTaiLieuModal(idCongViec);
                            }
                            return;
                        }

                        var btn = e.target.closest('button[data-action]');
                        if (!btn) return;
                        var action = btn.dataset.action;
                        var id = btn.dataset.id;
                        // So sánh id an toàn (string vs string)
                        var row = state.tasks.find(function(x) { return String(x.id) === String(id); });
                        if (!row) return;

                        try {
                            if (action === 'edit') {
                                fillTaskForm(row);
                                return;
                            }
                            if (action === 'delete') {
                                if (state.isLockedMonth) throw new Error('Tháng đã khóa, không thể xóa');
                                if (!confirm('Xóa công việc: ' + row.title + '?')) return;
                                await service.deleteTask(state.employee.msnv, state.selectedMonth, id);
                                await loadTasksBySelected();
                                resetTaskForm();
                                showToast('Đã xóa công việc', 'success');
                            }
                        } catch (err) {
                            logError(err);
                            showToast(err.message || 'Thao tác thất bại', 'error');
                        }
                    });
                }

                var btnSummarySubmit = byId('btnSummarySubmit');
                if (btnSummarySubmit) {
                    // Disable initially until tasks are loaded
                    btnSummarySubmit.disabled = true;

                    btnSummarySubmit.addEventListener('click', async function() {
                        var btn = this;

                        try {
                            // A) Validate
                            // Bỏ check isLockedMonth - cho phép tổng kết mọi tháng

                            // Use tasks from Tổng Kết tab (loaded via btnLoadTongKetTasks)
                            var tasks = state.tongketTasks || [];
                            var selectedMonth = byId('kpiMonth') ? byId('kpiMonth').value : '';

                            if (!selectedMonth) throw new Error('Vui lòng chọn tháng KPI');
                            if (tasks.length === 0) throw new Error('Chưa tải công việc. Vui lòng bấm "Tải danh sách công việc" trước.');

                            var empMeta = getEmployeeMetaForWork();
                            if (!empMeta || !empMeta.MSNV || !empMeta.HovaTen) throw new Error('Chưa có thông tin nhân viên');

                            // Parse month parts
                            var monthParts = getSelectedYearMonthParts(selectedMonth);

                            // B) Disable button trong lúc xử lý
                            btn.disabled = true;
                            showToast('Đang tổng kết...', 'info');

                            // C) Use already loaded tasks from Tổng Kết tab
                            // Already have tasks from state.tongketTasks

                            // D) Show confirm
                            if (!confirm('Đã tổng kết xong. Bạn có muốn mở Báo Cáo Tổng Hợp không?')) {
                                btn.disabled = false;
                                return;
                            }

                            // E) Fetch TyTrong by Group from Template
                            var tyTrongMap = await fetchTyTrongByGroupFromTemplate(empMeta);
                            logDebug('[SUMMARY] TyTrong map from template:', tyTrongMap);

                            // F) Build model cho report (theo mẫu BaoCaoTongHop_KyOnline_Mau_v4.html)
                            // Raw API response format: { HovaTen, MSNV, NhomCongViec, CongViec, ThoiHan, DienGiaiKetQua, TrangThai, ... }
                            var totalWeight = 0;

                            // Build groupMeta from tasks and tyTrongMap
                            var groupMeta = {};
                            var seenGroupNames = {};

                            tasks.forEach(function(t) {
                                var gName = t.NhomCongViec || t.groupName || 'Khác';
                                if (!seenGroupNames[gName]) {
                                    seenGroupNames[gName] = true;
                                    groupMeta[gName] = {
                                        tyTrongMau: Number(tyTrongMap[gName] || 0),
                                        nvTyTrong: '',
                                        qlTyTrong: '',
                                        qlDanhGia: ''
                                    };
                                }
                            });

                            // Calculate totalWeight: use tyTrongMau if available, else fallback to tasks.length
                            var sumTyTrong = 0;
                            Object.keys(groupMeta).forEach(function(gName) {
                                sumTyTrong += groupMeta[gName].tyTrongMau;
                            });

                            if (sumTyTrong &gt; 0) {
                                totalWeight = sumTyTrong;
                            } else {
                                // Fallback: count tasks
                                tasks.forEach(function(t) {
                                    totalWeight += 1;
                                });
                            }

                            var doneWeight = 0;
                            tasks.forEach(function(t) {
                                var s = (t.TrangThai || t.status || '').toLowerCase();
                                if (s === 'hoàn thành' || s === 'done' || s === 'xong') {
                                    doneWeight += 1;
                                }
                            });
                            var doneWeightPct = totalWeight &gt; 0 ? Math.round((doneWeight / totalWeight) * 100) : 0;

                            var groupCount = 0;
                            var seenGroups = {};
                            tasks.forEach(function(t) {
                                var gName = t.NhomCongViec || t.groupName || 'Khác';
                                if (!seenGroups[gName]) {
                                    seenGroups[gName] = true;
                                    groupCount++;
                                }
                            });

                            var now = new Date();
                            var createdDate = ('0' + now.getDate()).slice(-2) + '/' + ('0' + (now.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + '/' + now.getFullYear();

                            var emp = state.employee || {};
                            var model = {
                                period: selectedMonth,
                                createdDate: createdDate,
                                employee: {
                                    hoTen: emp.hoTen || empMeta.HovaTen || '',
                                    msnv: emp.msnv || empMeta.MSNV || '',
                                    phongBan: emp.phongBan || empMeta.PhongBan || '',
                                    email: emp.email || empMeta.Email || state.currentUserEmail || '',
                                    qlttEmail: emp.qlttEmail || empMeta.EmailQuanLy || state.currentUserEmail || '',
                                    chiNhanh: emp.chiNhanh || empMeta.ChiNhanh || '',
                                    chucVu: emp.chucVu || ''
                                },
                                tasks: tasks,
                                metrics: {
                                    totalTasks: tasks.length,
                                    totalWeight: totalWeight,
                                    doneWeightPct: doneWeightPct,
                                    groupCount: groupCount
                                },
                                groupMeta: groupMeta,
                                tyTrongByGroup: tyTrongMap
                            };

                            // F) Save pending TongKet model and meta
                            state.pendingTongKetModel = model;
                            state.pendingTongKetMeta = {
                                idTongKet: uid(),
                                thang: monthParts.Thang,
                                nam: monthParts.Nam,
                                empMeta: empMeta
                            };

                            // G) Render + open modal
                            var html = renderBaoCaoTongHopHTML(model);
                            baoCaoModal.open(html);

                        } catch (err) {
                            logError(err);
                            showToast(err.message || 'Tổng kết thất bại', 'error', 3500);
                        } finally {
                            // H) Finally: enable lại button
                            btn.disabled = false;
                        }
                    });
                }

                var btnReloadSummary = byId('btnReloadSummary');
                if (btnReloadSummary) btnReloadSummary.addEventListener('click', loadSummaryList);

                // Event delegation: click row in summary table to view TongKet detail
                var summaryTableBody = byId('summaryTableBody');
                if (summaryTableBody) {
                    summaryTableBody.addEventListener('click', async function(e) {
                        // Skip if click on button/link/input/textarea/select/label
                        if (e.target.closest('button, a, input, textarea, select, label')) return;

                        var tr = e.target.closest('tr');
                        if (!tr) return;

                        var idTongKet = (tr.dataset.idTongKet || '').trim();
                        if (!idTongKet) {
                            showToast('Không có IDTongKet để xem nội dung.', 'warn', 2500);
                            return;
                        }

                        // Loading UX
                        tr.classList.add('is-loading');
                        try {
                            var empMeta = getEmployeeMetaForWork();
                            var monthVal = (byId('kpiMonth') &amp;&amp; byId('kpiMonth').value || '').trim();
                            var monthParts = monthVal ? getSelectedYearMonthParts(monthVal) : null;

                            var payload = buildTongKetPayloadForNoiDung(empMeta, idTongKet, monthParts);
                            // Sanitize payload before API call
                            payload = sanitizePowerAutomatePayload(payload);

                            var raw = await callTongKetSignApi(payload);
                            var html = extractTongKetHtml(raw);

                            if (!html) throw new Error('API không trả về nội dung TongKet.');

                            // Save viewing state for handleSign to use
                            state.viewingTongKetId = idTongKet;
                            state.viewingTongKetEmpMeta = empMeta;

                            // Open modal with HTML
                            baoCaoModal.open(html);

                        } catch (err) {
                            showToast(err &amp;&amp; err.message || 'Không tải được nội dung tổng kết.', 'error', 3500);
                        } finally {
                            tr.classList.remove('is-loading');
                        }
                    });
                }

            }  // end bindEvents

            // ========================================================
            // === MODAL ADAPTER (Copy từ BangKiemQuyTrinh) ===
            // ========================================================
            function makeModalAdapter(el) {
                let bsInstance = null;
                if (window.bootstrap &amp;&amp; window.bootstrap.Modal) {
                    bsInstance = new bootstrap.Modal(el, { backdrop: true, keyboard: true });
                }

                function ensureBackdrop(show) {
                    const cls = 'modal-backdrop';
                    let bd = document.querySelector('.' + cls);
                    if (show) {
                        if (!bd) {
                            bd = document.createElement('div');
                            bd.className = cls + ' show';
                            bd.style.zIndex = '1050';
                            document.body.appendChild(bd);

                            // FIX: Only close modal if click is actually on backdrop, not inside modal content
                            bd.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                if (e.target === bd) {
                                    const modalContent = el.querySelector('.modal-content');
                                    if (modalContent &amp;&amp; !modalContent.contains(e.target)) {
                                        adapter.hide();
                                    } else if (!modalContent) {
                                        if (!el.contains(e.target)) {
                                    adapter.hide();
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            });

                            // Stop propagation from modal content to backdrop
                            const modalContent = el.querySelector('.modal-content');
                            if (modalContent) {
                                modalContent.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
                                    e.stopPropagation();
                                }, true);
                                modalContent.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
                                    e.stopPropagation();
                                }, true);
                            }
                        }
                    } else if (bd) {
                        bd.parentNode.removeChild(bd);
                    }
                }

                function handleEscKey(event) {
                    if (event.key === 'Escape' &amp;&amp; el.classList.contains('show')) {
                        adapter.hide();
                    }
                }

                const adapter = {
                    show() {
                        if (bsInstance) {
                            bsInstance.show();
                            return;
                        }

                        el.classList.add('show');
                        el.style.display = 'block';
                        el.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
                        el.style.zIndex = '1055';
                        document.body.classList.add('modal-open');
                        ensureBackdrop(true);
                        document.addEventListener('keydown', handleEscKey);
                        el.focus();
                    },
                    hide() {
                        if (bsInstance) {
                            bsInstance.hide();
                            return;
                        }

                        el.classList.remove('show');
                        el.style.display = 'none';
                        el.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                        document.body.classList.remove('modal-open');
                        ensureBackdrop(false);
                        document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleEscKey);
                    },
                    onShown(cb) {
                        if (bsInstance) {
                            el.addEventListener('shown.bs.modal', cb);
                        } else {
                            setTimeout(cb, 100);
                        }
                    }
                };

                // Bind all close buttons
                const closeBtns = el.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-dismiss="modal"]');
                closeBtns.forEach(btn =&gt; {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', () =&gt; adapter.hide());
                });

                return adapter;
            }

            // ========================================================
            // === BAO CAO MODAL OBJECT ===
            // ========================================================
            const baoCaoModal = {
                modalEl: document.getElementById('baoCaoTongHopModal'),
                modal: null,
                content: document.getElementById('baoCaoTongHopContent'),
                message: document.getElementById('baoCaoTongHopMessage'),

                init: function() {
                    this.modal = makeModalAdapter(this.modalEl);
                },

                open: function(html) {
                    if (!this.content) {
                        logError('baoCaoModal: content element not found');
                        return;
                    }

                    // Set HTML content
                    this.content.innerHTML = html;

                    // Clear message
                    if (this.message) {
                        this.message.innerHTML = '';
                    }

                    // Bind events for buttons inside the HTML
                    this.bindButtonEvents();

                    // Show modal
                    if (this.modal) {
                    this.modal.show();
                    }
                },

                bindButtonEvents: function() {
                    var self = this;

                    // Nút Ký
                    var signBtn = this.content.querySelector('.actions .btn');
                    if (signBtn &amp;&amp; signBtn.textContent.indexOf('KÝ') !== -1) {
                        // Replace onclick handler
                        signBtn.onclick = function() {
                            self.handleSign();
                        };
                    }

                    // Nút In - tìm button thứ 2 trong .actions
                    var actionBtns = this.content.querySelectorAll('.actions .btn');
                    if (actionBtns.length &gt;= 2) {
                        var printBtn = actionBtns[1];
                        if (printBtn &amp;&amp; printBtn.textContent.indexOf('IN') !== -1) {
                            printBtn.onclick = function() {
                                self.handlePrint();
                            };
                        }
                    }
                },

                handleSign: async function() {
                    var self = this;

                    // 1. Confirm before signing
                    if (!confirm('Xác nhận Lưu và Ký báo cáo tổng kết này?')) {
                        return;
                    }

                    // 2. Get current user email
                    var currentEmail = getCurrentUserEmail();
                    if (!currentEmail) {
                        showToast('Không xác định được user đăng nhập. Vui lòng đăng nhập lại.', 'error', 3000);
                        return;
                    }

                    // 3. Determine IDTongKet, empMeta, and monthParts
                    // Priority: viewing from list (state.viewingTongKetId) vs NV pending (state.pendingTongKetMeta)
                    var idTongKet = state.viewingTongKetId || (state.pendingTongKetMeta &amp;&amp; state.pendingTongKetMeta.idTongKet);
                    var empMeta = state.viewingTongKetEmpMeta || (state.pendingTongKetMeta &amp;&amp; state.pendingTongKetMeta.empMeta) || getEmployeeMetaForWork();

                    if (!empMeta) {
                        showToast('Không lấy được thông tin nhân viên.', 'error', 3000);
                        return;
                    }

                    // Get month parts from current dropdown or from meta
                    var monthVal = byId('kpiMonth') ? byId('kpiMonth').value.trim() : '';
                    var monthParts = monthVal ? getSelectedYearMonthParts(monthVal) : null;
                    if (!monthParts &amp;&amp; state.pendingTongKetMeta) {
                        monthParts = { Thang: state.pendingTongKetMeta.thang, Nam: state.pendingTongKetMeta.nam };
                    }

                    // 4. Determine role: NV or QL
                    var role = null;
                    var empEmail = (empMeta.Email || '').toLowerCase();
                    var empEmailQL = (empMeta.EmailQuanLy || '').toLowerCase();

                    if (empEmail === currentEmail) {
                        role = 'NV';
                    } else if (empEmailQL === currentEmail) {
                        role = 'QL';
                    } else {
                        showToast('Bạn không có quyền ký hồ sơ này.', 'warn', 3000);
                        return;
                    }

                    // 5. Collect groupMeta from group-rows (instead of individual task rows)
                    var htmlReport = '';
                    if (state.pendingTongKetModel) {
                        // NV: Collect groupMeta from group-rows
                        var groupRows = this.content.querySelectorAll('table.tasks tbody tr.group-row');

                        // Ensure groupMeta exists
                        if (!state.pendingTongKetModel.groupMeta) {
                            state.pendingTongKetModel.groupMeta = {};
                        }

                        groupRows.forEach(function(groupRow) {
                            var groupName = groupRow.dataset.group;
                            if (!groupName) return;

                            var nvTyTrongInput = groupRow.querySelector('input.ty-trong-nv');
                            var qlTyTrongInput = groupRow.querySelector('input.ty-trong-ql');
                            var mgrTextarea = groupRow.querySelector('textarea.mgr');

                            var nvTyTrong = nvTyTrongInput ? nvTyTrongInput.value.trim() : '';
                            var qlTyTrong = qlTyTrongInput ? qlTyTrongInput.value.trim() : '';
                            var qlDanhGia = mgrTextarea ? mgrTextarea.value.trim() : '';

                            // Update groupMeta
                            state.pendingTongKetModel.groupMeta[groupName] = {
                                tyTrongMau: state.pendingTongKetModel.groupMeta[groupName] ? state.pendingTongKetModel.groupMeta[groupName].tyTrongMau : 0,
                                nvTyTrong: nvTyTrong,
                                qlTyTrong: qlTyTrong,
                                qlDanhGia: qlDanhGia
                            };
                        });

                        // Re-render HTML with updated groupMeta
                        htmlReport = renderBaoCaoTongHopHTML(state.pendingTongKetModel);
                    } else {
                        // QL viewing from list: get HTML from current modal content
                        var wrap = this.content.querySelector('.wrap');
                        htmlReport = wrap ? wrap.outerHTML : this.content.innerHTML;
                    }

                    // 6. Build payload for Duyet
                    var payload = buildTongKetPayloadForDuyet(role, empMeta, idTongKet, monthParts, htmlReport);
                    payload = sanitizePowerAutomatePayload(payload);

                    // 7. Disable nút Ký để tránh double click
                    var signBtn = this.content.querySelector('.actions .btn');
                    if (signBtn) {
                        signBtn.disabled = true;
                        signBtn.innerHTML = '&lt;span class="ic"&gt;⏳&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="lbl"&gt;Đang ký...&lt;/span&gt;';
                    }

                    showToast('Đang Lưu và Ký...', 'info', 2000);

                    try {
                        // 8. Call TongKet Sign API
                        await callTongKetSignApi(payload);

                        // 9. Success
                        showToast('Đã Lưu và Ký tổng kết', 'success', 2500);

                        // 10. Refresh summary list
                        await loadSummaryList();

                        // 11. Reload content if viewing from list
                        if (state.viewingTongKetId) {
                            // Reload NoiDungTongKet to update badge status
                            var payloadView = buildTongKetPayloadForNoiDung(empMeta, idTongKet, monthParts);
                            payloadView = sanitizePowerAutomatePayload(payloadView);
                            var raw = await callTongKetSignApi(payloadView);
                            var htmlNew = extractTongKetHtml(raw);
                            if (htmlNew) {
                                this.content.innerHTML = htmlNew;
                            }
                        } else {
                            // NV: close modal after success
                            this.close();
                        }

                    } catch (err) {
                        logError(err);
                        // Re-enable nút Ký nếu có lỗi
                        if (signBtn) {
                            signBtn.disabled = false;
                            signBtn.innerHTML = '&lt;span class="ic"&gt;✍️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="lbl"&gt;LƯU &amp; KÝ&lt;/span&gt;';
                        }
                        showToast(err.message || 'Ký thất bại', 'error', 3500);
                    }
                },

                handlePrint: function() {
                    // Mở cửa sổ print riêng chỉ chứa report HTML
                    var printWindow = window.open('', '_blank', 'width=800,height=600');
                    if (!printWindow) {
                        alert('Không mở được cửa sổ in. Vui lòng cho phép popups.');
                        return;
                    }

                    // Lấy CSS từ content
                    var styles = this.content.querySelector('style');
                    var styleHTML = styles ? styles.outerHTML : '';

                    // Lấy nội dung wrap
                    var wrap = this.content.querySelector('.wrap');
                    var wrapHTML = wrap ? wrap.outerHTML : this.content.innerHTML;

                    // Build print HTML
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;html&gt;&lt;head&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;meta charset="utf-8"&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;title&gt;In Báo Cáo Tổng Hợp&lt;/title&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write(styleHTML);
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;style&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write('body { margin: 0; padding: 20px; }');
                    printWindow.document.write('@media print { .actions { display: none !important; } }');
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;/style&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write('&lt;/head&gt;&lt;body&gt;');
                    printWindow.document.write(wrapHTML);
                                printWindow.document.write('&lt;/body&gt;&lt;/html&gt;');
                                printWindow.document.close();

                    // Wait for content to load then print
                    printWindow.onload = function() {
                                printWindow.print();
                    };
                },

                close: function() {
                    // Reset viewing state when closing modal
                    state.viewingTongKetId = null;
                    state.viewingTongKetEmpMeta = null;

                    if (this.modal) {
                        this.modal.hide();
                    }
                },

                showMessage: function(msg, type) {
                    if (!this.message) return;

                    const alertClass = type === 'error' ? 'alert-danger' :
                                       type === 'success' ? 'alert-success' :
                                       type === 'warning' ? 'alert-warning' : 'alert-info';

                    this.message.innerHTML = '&lt;div class="alert ' + alertClass + '"&gt;' + msg + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                },

                showError: function(msg) {
                    this.showMessage(msg, 'error');
                },

                showLoading: function() {
                    if (this.content) {
                        this.content.innerHTML = '&lt;div class="text-center p-4"&gt;&lt;i class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin"&gt;&lt;/i&gt; Đang tải...&lt;/div&gt;';
                    }
                }
            };

            // ========================================================
            // === RENDER BAO CAO TONG HOP HTML ===
            // ========================================================
            const DEBUG_REPORT = false;

            function renderBaoCaoTongHopHTML(model) {
                // model = { period, createdDate, employee: {hoTen, msnv, phongBan, email, qlttEmail, chiNhanh, chucVu}, tasks: [], metrics: {totalTasks, totalWeight, doneWeightPct, groupCount}, groupMeta: {}, tyTrongByGroup: {} }

                var period = model.period || '';
                var createdDate = model.createdDate || '';
                var emp = model.employee || {};
                var tasks = model.tasks || [];
                var metrics = model.metrics || {};

                // Format tháng hiển thị
                var periodDisplay = period;
                if (period &amp;&amp; period.length &gt;= 7) {
                    var parts = period.split('-');
                    if (parts.length === 2) {
                        periodDisplay = 'Tháng ' + parseInt(parts[1]) + '/' + parts[0];
                    }
                }

                // Tính toán metrics
                var totalTasks = metrics.totalTasks || tasks.length;
                var totalWeight = metrics.totalWeight || 0;
                var doneWeightPct = metrics.doneWeightPct || 0;
                var groupCount = metrics.groupCount || 0;

                // ========== HELPER: Normalize task for report ==========
                function normalizeReportTask(t) {
                    return {
                        groupName: t.groupName || t.NhomCongViec || t.TenNhom || 'Khác',
                        title: t.title || t.CongViec || t.taskTitle || t.TenCongViec || '',
                        target: t.target || t.DienGiaiKetQua || t.dienGiaiKetQua || t.DienGiai || '',
                        status: t.status || t.TrangThai || t.trangThai || 'Mới',
                        danhGia: t.danhGia || t.DanhGia || t.danhGia || '',
                        files: t.attachmentUrl || t.taiLieu || t.TaiLieu || '',
                        thoiHanRaw: t.thoiHan || t.ThoiHan || t.dueDate || t.HanHoanTat || ''
                    };
                }

                // ========== HELPER: Parse thời hạn ==========
                function parseThoiHan(thoiHanRaw) {
                    var result = { fromDate: '', toDate: '' };
                    if (!thoiHanRaw || typeof thoiHanRaw !== 'string') return result;

                    var str = thoiHanRaw.trim();
                    // Try to split by common separators: ; | \n or "đến"/"-&gt;"/"-"&gt;"
                    var parts = str.split(/[;\n|]+/).map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(function(s) { return s; });

                    if (parts.length &gt;= 2) {
                        // 2 parts: from and to
                        result.fromDate = parseOneDate(parts[0]);
                        result.toDate = parseOneDate(parts[1]);
                    } else if (parts.length === 1) {
                        // Try patterns like "15/03/2025" or "2025-03-15"
                        // or patterns like "Từ 15/03 đến 20/03"
                        var singleStr = parts[0];
                        // Check if contains "đến" or "-&gt;" or "-"
                        var rangeMatch = singleStr.match(/(?:từ|from)\s*(\d{1,2}[\/\-]\d{2}[\/\-]?\d{0,4})\s*(?:đến|to|\-)\s*(\d{1,2}[\/\-]\d{2}[\/\-]?\d{0,4})/i);
                        if (rangeMatch) {
                            result.fromDate = parseOneDate(rangeMatch[1]);
                            result.toDate = parseOneDate(rangeMatch[2]);
                        } else {
                            // Single date - treat as "Đến ngày"
                            result.toDate = parseOneDate(singleStr);
                        }
                    }

                    return result;
                }

                function parseOneDate(dateStr) {
                    if (!dateStr || typeof dateStr !== 'string') return '';
                    var s = dateStr.trim();
                    // DD/MM/YYYY or D/M/YYYY
                    var dmMatch = s.match(/^(\d{1,2})[\/\-](\d{1,2})[\/\-](\d{2,4})$/);
                    if (dmMatch) {
                        var d = dmMatch[1];
                        var m = dmMatch[2];
                        var y = dmMatch[3];
                        if (y.length === 2) y = '20' + y;
                        return d.padStart(2, '0') + '/' + m.padStart(2, '0') + '/' + y;
                    }
                    // YYYY-MM-DD
                    var ymdMatch = s.match(/^(\d{4})[\/\-](\d{1,2})[\/\-](\d{1,2})$/);
                    if (ymdMatch) {
                        return ymdMatch[3].padStart(2, '0') + '/' + ymdMatch[2].padStart(2, '0') + '/' + ymdMatch[1];
                    }
                    return s; // Return as-is if can't parse
                }

                // ========== HELPER: Parse files ==========
                function parseFiles(filesStr) {
                    if (!filesStr || typeof filesStr !== 'string') return [];
                    // Split by ; or , or newlines
                    return filesStr.split(/[;\n,]+/).map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(function(s) { return s; });
                }

                // Nhóm tasks theo groupName (đã normalize)
                var groupedTasks = {};
                tasks.forEach(function(t) {
                    var nt = normalizeReportTask(t);
                    var gName = nt.groupName;
                    if (!groupedTasks[gName]) groupedTasks[gName] = [];
                    groupedTasks[gName].push(nt);
                });

                // HTML với scoped CSS
                var html = '';

                // 1. Scoped CSS
                html += '&lt;style&gt;';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent {';
                html += '  --brand:#f57c00; --brand-2:#ff9a3d; --ink:#111827; --muted:#6b7280;';
                html += '  --bg:#fff7ed; --card:#ffffff; --line:#e5e7eb; --ok:#16a34a; --wait:#f59e0b;';
                html += '  --soft:#fff3e0; --soft2:#fffaf5;';
                html += '  font-family: Montserrat, system-ui, -apple-system, Segoe UI, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif;';
                html += '  color: var(--ink);';
                html += '  background: linear-gradient(180deg, var(--bg), #fff 60%);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent * { box-sizing: border-box; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .wrap { max-width: 1100px; margin: 0 auto; padding: 16px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .banner {';
                html += '  background: linear-gradient(90deg, var(--brand), var(--brand-2)); color: #fff;';
                html += '  border-radius: 18px; padding: 18px; box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(245,124,0,.20);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .topbar { display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start; gap: 12px; flex-wrap: wrap; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .banner h1 { margin: 0; font-size: 20px; letter-spacing: .2px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .banner .sub { margin-top: 6px; font-size: 13px; opacity: .95; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .actions { display: flex; gap: 10px; align-items: center; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .btn {';
                html += '  appearance: none; border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.55); background: rgba(255,255,255,.12);';
                html += '  color: #fff; padding: 10px 14px; border-radius: 14px; font-weight: 700;';
                html += '  cursor: pointer; display: inline-flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center; justify-content: center;';
                html += '  gap: 6px; min-width: 64px; line-height: 1;';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .btn:hover { background: rgba(255,255,255,.18); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .btn:active { transform: translateY(1px); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .btn .ic { font-size: 18px; line-height: 1; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .btn .lbl { font-size: 12px; font-weight: 800; letter-spacing: .2px; line-height: 1; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .grid { display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1.05fr .95fr; gap: 14px; margin-top: 14px; }';
                html += '@media (max-width: 900px) { #baoCaoTongHopContent .grid { grid-template-columns: 1fr; } }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .card {';
                html += '  background: var(--card); border: 1px solid var(--line); border-radius: 18px; padding: 14px;';
                html += '  box-shadow: 0 6px 20px rgba(17,24,39,.06);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .card h2 { margin: 0 0 10px; font-size: 15px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .chips { display: flex; gap: 8px; flex-wrap: wrap; margin-top: 6px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .chip {';
                html += '  border: 1px solid var(--line); background: var(--soft2); border-radius: 999px;';
                html += '  padding: 6px 10px; font-size: 12px; color: var(--muted);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .chip b { color: var(--ink); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .mini { margin-top: 10px; display: grid; gap: 8px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .row {';
                html += '  display: flex; justify-content: space-between; gap: 10px; font-size: 13px;';
                html += '  border-top: 1px dashed var(--line); padding-top: 8px;';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .row .k { color: var(--muted); white-space: nowrap; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .row .v { text-align: right; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .metrics { display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr; gap: 10px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .kpi { border: 1px solid var(--line); border-radius: 14px; padding: 10px; background: #fff; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .kpi .v { font-weight: 700; font-size: 18px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .kpi .l { color: var(--muted); font-size: 12px; margin-top: 4px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .tablewrap { overflow: auto; border: 1px solid var(--line); border-radius: 16px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent table.tasks { width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-size: 13px; min-width: 1050px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent table.tasks th, #baoCaoTongHopContent table.tasks td { padding: 10px; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--line); vertical-align: top; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent table.tasks th { background: var(--soft); color: #7c2d12; font-weight: 700; text-align: left; position: sticky; top: 0; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent th .subhead { display: block; font-weight: 600; color: #9a3412; font-size: 11px; margin-top: 4px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .deadline { line-height: 1.25; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .deadline .lbl { display: block; color: var(--muted); font-size: 11px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent tr.group-row td { background: #fff; font-weight: 700; color: #7c2d12; border-bottom: 1px solid var(--line); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .group-pill {';
                html += '  display: inline-flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; padding: 6px 10px; border-radius: 999px;';
                html += '  background: var(--soft); border: 1px solid rgba(245,124,0,.25);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .att {';
                html += '  display: inline-flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px; border: 1px solid var(--line); background: #fff; border-radius: 999px;';
                html += '  padding: 4px 8px; font-size: 12px; color: var(--ink);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .att a { color: inherit; text-decoration: none; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .muted { color: var(--muted); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .resultcell .files { margin-top: 0px; display: flex; gap: 6px; flex-wrap: wrap; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .siggrid { display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr 1fr; gap: 12px; }';
                html += '@media (max-width: 900px) { #baoCaoTongHopContent .siggrid { grid-template-columns: 1fr; } }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .sig { border: 1px solid var(--line); border-radius: 18px; padding: 12px; background: #fff; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .sig .role { font-weight: 700; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .sig .who { margin-top: 6px; color: var(--muted); font-size: 12px; }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .sig .status { margin-top: 10px; display: inline-flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; padding: 6px 10px; border-radius: 999px; font-size: 12px; border: 1px solid var(--line); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .dot { width: 8px; height: 8px; border-radius: 999px; background: var(--wait); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .dot.ok { background: var(--ok); }';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .signbox {';
                html += '  margin-top: 10px; height: 92px; border: 1px dashed var(--line); border-radius: 14px;';
                html += '  display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; color: var(--muted); font-size: 12px; background: linear-gradient(180deg,#fff,#fafafa);';
                html += '}';
                html += '#baoCaoTongHopContent .footer { margin-top: 12px; color: var(--muted); font-size: 12px; }';
                html += '&lt;/style&gt;';

                // 2. Banner
                html += '&lt;div class="wrap"&gt;';
                html += '  &lt;div class="banner"&gt;';
                html += '    &lt;div class="topbar"&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;div&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;h1&gt;BÁO CÁO TỔNG HỢP CÔNG VIỆC ĐƯỢC KÝ DUYỆT&lt;/h1&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;div class="sub"&gt;Kỳ báo cáo: &lt;b&gt;' + periodDisplay + '&lt;/b&gt; và Ngày tạo: &lt;b&gt;' + createdDate + '&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;div class="actions"&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;button class="btn" type="button" onclick="onBaoCaoSignClick()"&gt;';
                html += '          &lt;span class="ic"&gt;✍️&lt;/span&gt;';
                html += '          &lt;span class="lbl"&gt;LƯU &amp; KÝ&lt;/span&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;/button&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;button class="btn" type="button" onclick="document.getElementById(\'baoCaoTongHopContent\').classList.add(\'printing\'); window.print();"&gt;';
                html += '          &lt;span class="ic"&gt;🖨️&lt;/span&gt;';
                html += '          &lt;span class="lbl"&gt;IN&lt;/span&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;/button&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '    &lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '  &lt;/div&gt;';

                // 3. Grid: Employee Info + Metrics
                html += '  &lt;div class="grid"&gt;';
                html += '    &lt;div class="card"&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;h2&gt;1) Thông tin nhân viên&lt;/h2&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;div class="chips"&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;div class="chip"&gt;&lt;b&gt;Nhân viên:&lt;/b&gt; ' + (emp.hoTen || '') + ' (' + (emp.msnv || '') + ')&lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;div class="chip"&gt;&lt;b&gt;BP:&lt;/b&gt; ' + (emp.phongBan || '') + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;div class="chip"&gt;&lt;b&gt;CN:&lt;/b&gt; ' + (emp.chiNhanh || '') + '&lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;div class="mini"&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;div class="row"&gt;&lt;div class="k"&gt;Email&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="v"&gt;&lt;b&gt;' + (emp.email || '') + '&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '        &lt;div class="row"&gt;&lt;div class="k"&gt;Quản lý trực tiếp&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="v"&gt;&lt;b&gt;' + (emp.qlttEmail || '') + '&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
                if (emp.chucVu) {
                    html += '        &lt;div class="row"&gt;&lt;div class="k"&gt;Chức vụ&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="v"&gt;&lt;b&gt;' + emp.chucVu + '&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
                }
                html += '      &lt;/div&gt;';
                html += '    &lt;/div&gt;';

                html += '    &lt;div class="card"&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;h2&gt;2) Chỉ số tổng hợp&lt;/h2&gt;';
                html += '      &lt;div class="metrics"&gt;';
